          <h1>
           Classic Chevy &amp; GMC Truck Parts
          </h1>
          <p>
           Welcome to BrothersTrucks.com, America's #1 Source for 1947-87 Chevrolet &amp; GMC Truck Parts - Classic &amp; Custom. If you're looking for classic Chevy truck parts or classic GMC truck parts, we have 1000's of the highest quality classic truck parts you can find. Whether you're restoring an original or seeking custom classic truck parts, we're your source.
          </p>
          <p>
           Pick up a copy of our brand new
           <a href="/catalog-request.asp">
            catalog
           </a>
           , or browse new products and web specials. We also have a ton of
           <a href="http://blog.brotherstrucks.com/diy-articles">
            technical articles
           </a>
           with all you need to know about restoring your classic truck. And if you're looking for photos of classic Chevrolet &amp; GMC trucks, try our
           <a href="http://blog.brotherstrucks.com/view/truck-shows/">
            truck show galleries
           </a>
           .
          </p>
          <br/>
          <br/>

    $(document).ready(function(){
 		$("#accordian a").click(function(){
 			var link = $(this);
 			var closest_ul = link.closest("ul");
 			var parallel_active_links = closest_ul.find(".active")
 			var closest_li = link.closest("li");
 			var link_status = closest_li.hasClass("active");
 			var count = 0;
 
 			closest_ul.find("ul").slideUp(function(){
 				if(++count == closest_ul.find("ul").length)
 					parallel_active_links.removeClass("active");
 			});
 
 			if(!link_status)
 			{
 				closest_li.children("ul").slideDown();
 				closest_li.addClass("active");
 			}
 		})
 		
 		$( "#0" ).addClass( "active" );
 		$( "#0" ).addClass( "active" );
 		$( "#0" ).addClass( "active" );
 		$( "#0" ).addClass( "active" );
 		
 	})
   </script>
